| 0:26:38| This is actually set by state law.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=1598)|
| 0:26:41| It's a fairly complicated formula.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=1601)|
| 0:26:43| There are two parts to both of these electrical and gas.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=1603)|
| 0:26:48| One is basically the plant and inventory and equipment for KUB in each of these jurisdictions,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=1608)|
| 0:26:59| and that's why you'll see multiple jurisdictions because KUB has plant equipment in all of| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=1619)|
| 0:27:05| these jurisdictions.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=1625)|
| 0:27:06| Part two is a piece that's based on total operating revenue, less purchase power.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=1626)|
| 0:27:12| And for that, the city receives 77.5 percent of the part two distributions on electrical| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=1632)|
| 0:27:26| and 100 percent of the distributions on gas.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=1646)|

| 0:27:43| than that.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=1663)|

| 0:44:25| This area is flooded due to sinkholes and lack of drainage for over 40 years.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=2665)|

| 0:44:36| in Harrell Hills there are 11 active sinks.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=2676)|
| 0:44:40| Houses that were constructed in three of them.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=2680)|
| 0:44:44| Flooding occurs when storms produce runoff in excess of the ability of the sink,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=2684)|
| 0:44:50| an underlying cavern system into which it drains to carry off the flow.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=2690)|
| 0:44:56| There is no surface drainage from this area.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=2696)|
| 0:45:00| Capacity of the underground drainage system is exceeded during periods of heavy,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=2700)|

| 0:45:20| includes quantities of sediment.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=2720)|
| 0:45:23| Sinkholes can easily plug from sediment, trash, or debris,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=2723)|
| 0:45:26| as noted in the city's stormwater engineering policy 12.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=2726)|
| 0:45:30| Sinkholes may close because of land use changes or for no given reason,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=2730)|
| 0:45:37| and they should be considered very fragile.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=2737)|
| 0:45:40| Studies should be conducted before land use changes in the drainage area| [source video](https://archive.org/details/citycouncilr265130319?start=2740)|
